   function iqContentPlatformLoad(isArtikel) {
  var s = document.createElement('script');
  s.type = 'text/javascript';
  s.id = "iqContentPlatform";
  s.async = true;
  s.src = document.location.protocol + '//cdn.iqcontentplatform.de/iq.js';
  var sc = document.getElementsByTagName('script')[0]; sc.parentNode.insertBefore(s, sc);
  try { console.log("iqcontentplatform inserted "+(isArtikel?"Teaser":"Content"))} catch(e) {};  
}
(function() {
  var pathArr = location.pathname.split("/");
  if (location.hostname.indexOf("iqcontentplatform.de") &gt; -1 ||
  	(pathArr.length == 3 &amp;&amp; pathArr[1] == "anzeigen" &amp;&amp; pathArr[2].lastIndexOf(".html") == pathArr[2].length-5)) {
   	iqContentPlatformLoad(false);
  }    
})();

  <script type="text/javascript">
   jQuery("body").bind("iq-artikelanker", function () {
	try {
		console.log("iq-artikelanker triggered")
	} catch (e) {}
	if (jQuery("#iqContentPlatform").length == 0)
		iqContentPlatformLoad(true); // site-inject.js
});

jQuery(function () {
	try {
		console.log("iq-artikelanker analysis")
	} catch (e) {}

	var allPos = jQuery("#FAZContent DIV[itemprop=articleBody] &gt; DIV[class=''] &gt; p, #FAZContent DIV[itemprop=articleBody] &gt; DIV[class=''] &gt; h2").map(function () {
		return this
	}).get();
	var firstPos = 2;
	var lastPos = allPos.length - 1;
	var insertPos = -1;
	var isAdFree = false; // (typeof oAdvert == "undefined");
	var fazPath = location.pathname.split("/");
	var isStil = fazPath.length &gt;= 3 &amp;&amp; fazPath[2] == "stil";
	if (!isAdFree &amp;&amp; !isStil)
		jQuery(allPos).each(function (i) {
			if ((jQuery(this).next()[0] != undefined &amp;&amp; jQuery(this).prev()[0] != undefined)) {
				try {
					console.log("iq-artikelanker check: " + this.tagName + " (" + jQuery(this).attr("class") + "): " + i + ": next:" + jQuery(this).next()[0].tagName + ", prev:" + jQuery(this).prev()[0].tagName)
				} catch (e) {}
				var $next, $prev;
				var isNextOK = ($next=jQuery(this).next())[0].tagName in {"P": true, "H2": true} &amp;&amp;
					!($next.text() == "" || $next.hasClass("WeitereBeitraege") || $next.hasClass("AutorenModul"));
				var isPrevOK = ($prev=jQuery(this).prev())[0].tagName in {"P": true, "H2": true} &amp;&amp;
					!($prev.text() == "" || $prev.hasClass("WeitereBeitraege") || $prev.hasClass("AutorenModul"));
				if (i &gt;= firstPos &amp;&amp; i &lt;= lastPos &amp;&amp; isNextOK &amp;&amp; isPrevOK &amp;&amp; jQuery(this).attr("class") == undefined) {
					insertPos = i;
					try {
						console.log("iq-artikelanker position = " + i);
					} catch (e) {}
					return false;
				}
			}
		});

	// Drop Anchor
	jQuery(allPos[insertPos == -1 ? 0 : insertPos]).before("&lt;div id='iq-artikelanker'" + (insertPos == -1 ? "style='display:none'" : "") + "&gt;&lt;/div&gt;");
	if (insertPos &gt; -1)
		jQuery("body").trigger("iq-artikelanker");

	try {
		console.log("iq-artikelanker checked (" + allPos.length + "):" + (insertPos == -1 ? "no go" : "ok") + ", ads=" + (isAdFree ? "no" : "ok") + ", isStil=" + (isStil ? "ok" : "no"))
	} catch (e) {}
});
  </script>

        function trackTwitter(intent_event) {
            // The previous call
            __GETS.sotw(intent_event);
            if (intent_event) {
                var opt_pagePath;
                if (intent_event.target &amp;&amp; intent_event.target.nodeName == 'IFRAME') {
                    opt_target = extractParamFromUri(intent_event.target.src, 'url');
                }
                ga('send', {
                    'hitType': 'social',
                    'socialNetwork': 'Twitter',
                    'socialAction': 'Tweet',
                    'socialTarget': opt_pagePath,
                    'page': jQuery(document).attr('title')
                });
            }
        }

        function extractParamFromUri(uri, paramName) {
            if (!uri) {
                return;
            }
            var regex = new RegExp('[\\?&amp;#]' + paramName + '=([^&amp;#]*)');
            var params = regex.exec(uri);
            if (params != null) {
                return unescape(params[1]);
            }
            return;
        }

          <h2>
           <a class="TeaserHeadLink" href="/aktuell/beruf-chance/nine-to-five/kolumne-nine-to-five-der-sympathische-haendedruck-13694820.html" title="Kolumne Nine to five: Der sympathische Hndedruck">
            <span class="Stichwort">
             Kolumne Nine to five
            </span>
            <span class="Headline">
             Der sympathische Hndedruck
            </span>
           </a>
          </h2>
          <p class="Copy" title="Kolumne Nine to five: Der sympathische Hndedruck">
           <span class="TeaserText">
            Ein Kollege in unserem Bro begrt an jedem Morgen alle Kollegen mit einem Hndedruck. Ausnahmslos alle, mit einem Handschlag, mittelfest. Ohne ihn wrde etwas fehlen. Doch warum blo hat noch kein anderer Mitarbeiter diesen schnen Brauch bernommen?
           </span>
           <span class="mehrInfo">

          <h2>
           <a class="TeaserHeadLink" href="/aktuell/gesellschaft/menschen/smalltalk/britischer-saenger-george-michael-widerspricht-drogengeruechten-13689451.html" title="Britischer Snger: George Michael widerspricht Drogengerchten">
            <span class="Stichwort">
             Britischer Snger
            </span>
            <span class="Headline">
             George Michael widerspricht Drogengerchten
            </span>
           </a>
          </h2>
          <p class="Copy" title="Britischer Snger: George Michael widerspricht Drogengerchten">
           <span class="TeaserText">
            Der Snger George Michael verwahrt sich gegen Gerchte ber seine Drogensucht, Ingrid Steeger spricht ber traurige Kindheitserinnerungen, und Frst Albert II. will nach zehn Jahren auf dem Thron mehr ko statt Glamour  der Smalltalk.
           </span>

       <script type="text/javascript">
        function getSelectedValue(id) {
           return jQuery("#" + id).find(".sub span.value").html();
      }



jQuery( document ).ready(function() {
      jQuery('ul.level2 input[type="checkbox"]').click(function () {

          var selected = [];
          jQuery('.level2 input:checked').each(function() {
          if (jQuery(this).is(":checked")) { selected.push(jQuery(this).attr('id')); }
          });

          if (selected.length &gt; 0) {
              var dashtml = '&lt;span&gt;' + selected[0] + '&lt;/span&gt;';
              jQuery('.multiSel').html(dashtml);
              jQuery(".hF").hide();
          } 
          else {
          	  var dashtml = '&lt;span&gt;Newsletter auswhlen&lt;/span&gt;';
              jQuery('.multiSel').html(dashtml);
              jQuery(".hF").hide();             
          }
      });
      
      function validateEmail(email) {
         var re = /^([\w-]+(?:\.[\w-]+)*)@((?:[\w-]+\.)*\w[\w-]{0,66})\.([a-z]{2,6}(?:\.[a-z]{2})?)$/i;
         return re.test(email);}
      
      jQuery("#nlsubmit").submit(function(){
      	var theErr = '';
      	allok = 1;
      	email = jQuery( "input#themail" ).val();
      	laenge = jQuery(".level2 input[type='checkbox']:checked").length ;
      	theOptIn = jQuery( ".optInField input[type='checkbox']:checked" ).length;
        if (email == '')
         {
         theErr = "&lt;span&gt;Bitte geben Sie eine Mail-Adresse an.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br /&gt;";
         jQuery("#themail").addClass("ErrorData");
         allok = 0;
         } 
         else 
         {
         if (validateEmail(email)) {         	      	
         jQuery("#themail").removeClass("ErrorData");
         } else {
         theErr = "&lt;span&gt;Bitte geben Sie eine gltige Mail-Adresse an.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br /&gt;";
         allok = 0;
         }
         }        
         
        if (laenge &lt; 1) 
         {
         theErr += "&lt;span&gt;Bitte whlen Sie einen Newsletter aus.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br /&gt;";
         jQuery(".sub").addClass("ErrorData");
         allok = 0;
         }   
         else
         {
         jQuery(".sub").removeClass("ErrorData");
         }
          
        if (theOptIn != 1) 
         {
         theErr += "&lt;span&gt;Bitte akzeptieren Sie die Datenschutzerklrung.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br /&gt;";
         jQuery(".optInField").addClass("ErrorData");
         allok = 0;
         }
         else
         {
         jQuery(".optInField").removeClass("ErrorData");
         }
     
        
        if (allok == 1) {      	
         jQuery.ajax({ jsonpCallback: 'jsonCallback', contentType: "application/json", dataType: 'jsonp', url: 'http://dst.faz.net/nl-widget/submit.php', data:jQuery('#nlsubmit').serialize(), beforeSend: function () { jQuery('#nlsubmit').hide();jQuery('.NLSignUp .Headline').hide();$('#success').html("&lt;img src='http://www.faz.net/img/ajax-loader.gif' /&gt;");}, success: function(response){jQuery('#success').html( "&lt;span style='color:green;font-size:12px'&gt;"+response.ok+" &lt;/span&gt;").fadeIn(2000);}});
         
         }
         else
         {
          jQuery( "#success" ).empty().html(theErr);
          theErr = '';
         }
         
         
         return false;
       });
       
      
      
   });
       </script>
